  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_15784656-68a2-4d23-ab7e-12c515923ed9'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText11624582511913963018" style="display:none"><p>THE WAR IS OVER.</p><p></p><p>BUT THE TRUE HORROR HAS ONLY JUST BEGUN....</p><p></p><p>For more than six hundred years, Selene was a Death Dealer, a vampire warrior dedicated to the destruction of her people's savage enemies: the werewolves. But then she learned the shocking truth behind the ancient conflict and turned against her undead masters.</p><p></p><p>For all of his mortal life, Michael was an ordinary human, ignorant of the night's darkest mysteries -- until he found himself caught in the middle of a shadow war between immortal rivals. Bitten by both a lycan and a vampire, he has now become a hybrid creature whose ultimate potential remains unknown.</p><p></p><p>Together, Selene and Michael have become outcasts -- and targets, for a long-buried menace has risen from the depths of history in search of unholy vengeance. Now, in order to survive, Selene must uncover a terrible secret hidden deep within the shadows of her own forgotten past....</p><p></p></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17752774826368907546">This book is one of the best books of 2005. It has a great storyline and is full of action. When the movie comes out I look forward to seeing it. Greg Cox wrote a fantastic book version of the movie and I praise him for that. I recommend this book to anyone who enjoys the underworld series of books. This one takes the cake. I will not spoil it for anyone expect that Selene and Michael become closer and the action is bigger and more exciting.</span>

  <span id="freeText6453569360512792416" style="display:none">This book was incredible! Like most of the the Underworld books I couldn't stop reading. This book is ten times better than the first book. Love Selene And Michael. I can't wait to read more of Greg's books. I hope he publishes more books than just 4 book. <br /><br />I like to know what relationship trouble Selene and Michael will have. You tend to worry more about there survival than there love for one another. Even if you want to read more love between them, it all erases from ur memory when you read that there fight for there lives. It's so amazing. This is one of my favorite books. You know when you fall upon a great book and time passes and you haven't slept because ur to busy wondering what might happen next. <br /><br />I still wonder what might happen next after they pretty much killed everyone. I don't know how the book will continue on. I'd love to see more of Vicktor and his wife. I like to know who was Selene before she became a vampire. I know that Vicktor created her. But I want to know why she never shows any emotion. I know that some of the reason was because her family died and she thought for years that Lycan's killed then. But there has to be another reason. Did she have another love. I want to know why Viktor didn't kill her. He must of saw something in Selene maybe she reminded him of the daughter he once had. <br /><br />For this, Selene will be one character to remember. <br /></span>

            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3440540947" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13404014458876126222">E fu così che conclusi una delle più toccanti e complete minisaghe vamp/lica che mi sia mai capitato di leggere, vedere, assaporare ed amare come questa di Underworld. So che in un prossimo futuro ci sarà un continuo e spero sia apri ai precedenti e che possa in qualche modo leggerlo così come ho fatto con questi due episodi. So che c'è anche un prequel che accetto come sola visione, perchè deludente sotto certi punti di vista.<br/>Ma ora so chi sono veramente i protagonisti che ho amato sullo scherm</span>
  <span id="freeText13404014458876126222" style="display:none">E fu così che conclusi una delle più toccanti e complete minisaghe vamp/lica che mi sia mai capitato di leggere, vedere, assaporare ed amare come questa di Underworld. So che in un prossimo futuro ci sarà un continuo e spero sia apri ai precedenti e che possa in qualche modo leggerlo così come ho fatto con questi due episodi. So che c'è anche un prequel che accetto come sola visione, perchè deludente sotto certi punti di vista.<br />Ma ora so chi sono veramente i protagonisti che ho amato sullo schermo!<br />So cosa ha provato Michael in determinate situazioni, e cosa ha celato dietro il suo sguardo da dura Selene per poi cedere alle lacrime nei momenti dove era troppo forte il dolore, la passione o comunque quanto provava dentro di se.<br />In un bagno di sangue eterno, in uno specchiato cinematografico, in una lotta contro il tempo e contro la legge del più forte e del passato contro il futuro, si gioca la vita e la sopravvivenza di una vampira e un lyca allo stato ibrido.<br />Non occorre aggiungere altro, perchè Cox è riuscito a mantenersi estraneo alla vicenda e a lasciare che al storia e gli eventi parlassero da se. C'è solo una cosa che voglio dire: bello! Merita tutta l'angoscia che mi accompagna fino agli eventi futuri.<br /></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText9347819863839626442" style="display:none">I was pleased overall with this book. It really held true to the movie... didn’t introduce many new thoughts, but I liked that he didn’t try to change it too much from the movie. It was short and sweet, if a little less engaging than the first book/movie. (But that is the way I felt about the movie too. It was good but not as good as the first... or third for that matter). <br /><br />I do wish that there was a little more about Selene and Michael... But it was enough for me to be somewhat satisfied. I am glad he didn’t continue the series past movie three. I’m already disappointed with the way things went in the fourth and fifth movies... can’t imagine the books being very good. Overall it was fun!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15402372702756446834">This, the third book in the triology, brings the Underworld story to a conclusion. It's well written, the pacing is good throughout, and thankfully the characters are given more life here than in the movie. While I like the Underworld movies, and have read all three books, I'd have to plump for the books as being the better option. One reason for that is what I've stated previously, in that the book gives the characters more life--you get inside their heads and feel their emotions, something you</span>
  <span id="freeText15402372702756446834" style="display:none">This, the third book in the triology, brings the Underworld story to a conclusion. It's well written, the pacing is good throughout, and thankfully the characters are given more life here than in the movie. While I like the Underworld movies, and have read all three books, I'd have to plump for the books as being the better option. One reason for that is what I've stated previously, in that the book gives the characters more life--you get inside their heads and feel their emotions, something you can't do with a movie. The other plus with book over film, is you don't have to be subjected to Scott Speedman's god-awful acting.<br /><br />Do you read the book first, or watch the film? Won't matter, because the two intermesh, there's no plot additions in the novel version. If you read the book, you know what'll happen in the film and vice-versa. But that takes nothing away from this read; an excellent end to the Underworld trilogy and yes. . . Selene rocks!</span>

Surrounded by hacking coughs, screaming babies, and Sky Mall catalogs, I did my best to get into this novel. I failed.<br /><br />I'm unsure if my dislike of this book stems from the author's simplistic writing style or the way he conveys the characters inner thoughts and emotions. Maybe I should just be thankful his brevity enabled me to read the book in less time than it took to watch the movie.<br /><br />You can read the first two chapters on Amazon for free via their Peek Inside option. I kept hoping it would get better but it never did. Save your time and skip this book. The Sky Mall catalog was more enthralling.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17380072467858387747" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/i59Yg++9UoRyxD7k9R2NHQQRdw0EMgngTBgjLYtxjaXqPbC2HRKCiQNP0DMTKCKdypMf3jUHCxjjgx4aAhB4g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
